implementation:\\n- **source/common/http/header_map_impl.cc**: The HeaderMapImpl class stores all header names in lowercase through the Http::LowerCaseString wrapper, ensuring all headers are normalized to lowercase regardless of input case\\n- **source/common/http/http1/header_formatter.cc**: Provides header formatting utilities that maintain lowercase normalization when encoding/decoding HTTP/1 headers\\n- **source/extensions/http/header_validators/envoy_default/http1_header_validator.cc**: The ServerHttp1HeaderValidator::transformRequestHeaders() and ClientHttp1HeaderValidator::transformResponseHeaders() methods validate and normalize headers according to RFC 9110 and RFC 9112 specifications\\n\\n## Pseudo-Header Injection (:method, :path, :scheme, :authority, :protocol)\\n\\nThe pseudo-header handling is split between HTTP/2 codec and validators:\\n- **source/common/http/http2/codec_impl.cc**: The HTTP/2 codec implementation injects and handles pseudo-headers during frame encoding/decoding. The encodeHeadersBase() method constructs HTTP/2 HEADERS frames with proper pseudo-header placement\\n- **source/extensions/http/header_validators/envoy_default/http2_header_validator.cc**: The Http2HeaderValidator class implements comprehensive pseudo-header validation in validateRequestHeaders(). The ServerHttp2HeaderValidator::transformRequestHeaders() and ClientHttp2HeaderValidator::transformRequestHeaders() methods handle the injection of :method, :path, :scheme, and :authority pseudo-headers. These functions manage Connection, Upgrade headers and convert them to HTTP/2 pseudo-headers\\n- **source/extensions/http/header_validators/envoy_default/http2_header_validator.cc**: Implements upgrade request/response validation and transformation in ServerHttp2HeaderValidator and ClientHttp2HeaderValidator classes. Special handling for extended CONNECT protocol negotiation\\n- **source/common/http/headers.h**: Defines standard upgrade header constants (websocket, h2c, connect-udp, etc.)\\n- **source/extensions/http/header_validators/envoy_default/config_overrides.h**: Manages runtime configuration for upgrade handling behavior\\n\\n## Processing Pipeline\\n\\nThe complete header translation pipeline flows as follows:\\n1. HTTP/1 requests are parsed by source/common/http/http1/codec_impl.cc (using balsa_parser.cc or legacy_parser_impl.cc)\\n2. Raw headers are stored in HeaderMapImpl (source/common/http/header_map_impl.cc) with automatic lowercase normalization\\n3. Headers pass through ServerHttp1HeaderValidator::transformRequestHeaders() (source/extensions/http/header_validators/envoy_default/http1_header_validator.cc) for validation and potential upgrade transformation\\n4. For HTTP/2 upstreams, utility functions in source/common/http/utility.cc perform protocol conversion (transformUpgradeRequestFromH1toH2)\\n5. The HTTP/2 codec in source/common/http/http2/codec_impl.cc receives the transformed headers with pseudo-headers\\n6. ServerHttp2HeaderValidator and ClientHttp2HeaderValidator (source/extensions/http/header_validators/envoy_default/http2_header_validator.cc) validate and finalize pseudo-header placement\\n7. HTTP/2 HEADERS frames are encoded with proper pseudo-header ordering per RFC 7540\\n\\nThe reverse path (HTTP/2 to HTTP/1) follows the same pattern in reverse using transformUpgradeRequestFromH2toH1 and transformUpgradeResponseFromH2toH1.\\n\\nKey architectural features:\\n- **Automatic lowercase normalization** via Http::LowerCaseString in HeaderMapImpl\\n- **RFC compliance** through separate validators for HTTP/1 (RFC 9112) and HTTP/2 (RFC 7540/RFC 9114)\\n- **Extensible validation** via HeaderValidatorFactory and pluggable validator implementations\\n- **Protocol-agnostic internal representation** where HTTP/2 concepts (pseudo-headers) are the canonical form\\n- **Upgrade handling** for WebSocket, CONNECT, and H2C protocols with proper header transformation\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
